abrahamic_group = {
	graphical_culture = muslimgfx
	playable = yes
	has_coa_on_barony_only = yes
	hostile_within_group = yes

	ai_convert_same_group = 1 # try to convert if ai_zeal is high
	ai_convert_other_group = 2 # always try to convert
	
	# Reformed

	judaism_reformed = {
		allow_in_ruler_designer = no
		graphical_culture = jewishgfx
		color = { 0.5 1 0.8 }
		icon = 56
		heresy_icon = 57
		
		high_god_name = GOD_YAHWEH
		
		piety_name = PIETY
		priest_title = RABBI
		scripture_name = THE_TORAH
		god_names = {
			 GOD_YAHWEH ADONAI PROPHET_MOSES
		}
		evil_god_names = {
			SATAN
		}
		
		character_modifier = {
			global_revolt_risk = -0.03
			general_opinion = 10
			church_opinion = -10
			temple_vassal_tax_modifier = 0.10
			build_cost_modifier = -0.10
			land_organisation = 0.25
#			monthly_character_prestige = 1.20
			diplomacy = 1
			martial = -1
			stewardship = 3
			learning = -3
#			ai_ambition = 20
#			ai_zeal = 20
#			ai_honor = 60
#			ai_rationality = 50
		}
		unit_home_modifier = {
			key = "DEF_RELIGION"
			
			light_cavalry_defensive = 0.50
			light_infantry_defensive = 0.50
			archers_defensive = 0.50
			knights_defensive = 0.50
			heavy_infantry_defensive = 0.50
			pikemen_defensive = 0.50
			land_morale = 1.50
		}
		
		has_heir_designation = yes
		can_call_crusade = no
		raised_vassal_opinion_loss = no
		short_reign_opinion_year_mult = 2 # The default in LI is 5
		
		
		# Jewish restrictive (sectarian 1), can be married only from the same group or civilization
		intermarry = judaism
		intermarry = jud_ark_reformed
		
		religious_clothing_head = 12
		religious_clothing_priest = 12
		
	}
